There are some companies in the U.S. like Fervo which are doing well and claim to use new tech but they are still in the pipeline stage where the money is being raised for development/construction. ↵ On general energy wars, would say that Russia Ukraine war really fronted the energy security question with gas supply to Europe impacted and energy prices skyrocketing- it led to some countries focusing even more on renewables because own resources but shifted the conversation from climate change to security. Energy security though remains one of the top policy issues especially with growing data center demand and is a much more important issue in the top echelons than it would appear. Especially in countries like U.S. where energy talk is accompanied with conversations around renewables and increasing coal/natural gas and seems more of a cultural issue than a national security issue.
